         <div class="panel entry-content" id="tab-description">
          <h2>
           Product Description
          </h2>
          <p>
           <b>
            OG Kush Flavor
           </b>
          </p>
          <p>
           A Ganja Juice certified bestseller- the OG Kush Flavor e liquid features the potent piney taste made from natural fresh fruit extracts. This thrilling ecig liquid juice comes in a deep rich flavor without the harsh burn. Full satisfaction follows with every draw giving the pleasant effects similar to kush-weed that can give you the ultimate high from your vapor smoking.
          </p>
          <p>
           Ganja Juice is able to produce the highest quality e cigarette flavors refills that are carefully blended from entirely all U. S. made and produced ingredients to ensure premium flavors and excellent vapors that you can safely enjoy. Ganja ejuice is purely made from fresh fruit and herbal extracts using Food Grade USP Kosher Vegetable Glycerin (VG) and Food Grade USP Kosher Propylene Glycol (PG) with all natural and in some 100% organic food flavorings to provide you a smooth throaty hit while giving out strong large vapor cloud smoke. The 50/50 blend us ideal for all types or cartomizers, atomizers and tanks. Ganja Juice strives to be the best when it comes to ejuice vapor smoking and now a fastest growing e juice manufacturing company today. Our complete line of vapor smoking products are carefully handpicked and selected for the ultimate vape smoking experience that you truly deserve. Weve got you covered here when it comes to your e cig pleasure.
          </p>
          <p>
           Your pleasure is our business and that is why you are our priority. Just drop us a line or two and let us know of your pleasant vape experience or if you have something else on your mind. Comments are welcome here and we love to hear from you!
          </p>
          <p>
           <i>
            FYI: THESE DELICIOUS E-JUICE FLAVORS ARE PURELY INTENDED FOR FUN VAPE SMOKING AND ARE CONSIDERED AS NOVELTY ITEMS. NO ACTIVE SUBSTANCE OR INGREDIENTS WERE USED OTHER THAN THE DESIRED NICOTINE CONTENT.
           </i>
          </p>
